Default value : actionCreatorFactory('api')
ApiStoreActions
ApiStoreActions: object
Type : object
Default value : { RESET: actionCreator<null>('RESET'), RESET_ERRORS: actionCreator<null>('RESET_ERRORS'), RESET_SUCCESS: actionCreator<null>('RESET_SUCCESS'), STATE_LOADING: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('STATE_LOADING'), STATE_MODIFYING: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('STATE_MODIFYING'), STATE_ERROR: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('STATE_ERROR'), GET_COMPLETE: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('GET_COMPLETE'), POST_COMPLETE: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('POST_COMPLETE'), PUT_COMPLETE: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('PUT_COMPLETE'), UPSERT_COMPLETE: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('UPSERT_COMPLETE'), DELETE_COMPLETE: actionCreator<AppStore.ApiResponse>('DELETE_COMPLETE'), }

Api action
createEntity
createEntity:
Default value : <t>(uniqueId: string) => { const adapter = createEntityAdapter<t>({ selectId: entity => (<any>entity)[uniqueId] }); const state = adapter.getInitialState(<AppStore.ApiState<t>>{ loading: null, data: null, error: null, modifying: null, success: null, }); return { adapter: adapter, initialState: state, uniqueId: uniqueId, }; }

Returns an adapter, initial state and uniqueId for ngrx entity This is necessary to define the unique ID/primary key for each model
